    99	    public EventBus getOrCreateDefaultBus(String region) {
   100	        String key = busKey(region, "default");
   101	        return busStore.get(key).orElseGet(() -> {
   102	            EventBus bus = new EventBus(
   103	                    "default",
   104	                    regionResolver.buildArn("events", region, "event-bus/default"),
   105	                    null,
   106	                    Instant.now()
   107	            );
   108	            busStore.put(key, bus);
   109	            return bus;
   110	        });
   111	    }
   112	
   113	    public EventBus createEventBus(String name, String description,
   114	                                   Map<String, String> tags, String region) {
   115	        if (name == null || name.isBlank()) {
   116	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException", "EventBus name is required.", 400);
   117	        }
   118	        String key = busKey(region, name);
   119	        if (busStore.get(key).isPresent()) {
   120	            throw new AwsException("ResourceAlreadyExistsException",
   121	                    "EventBus already exists: " + name, 400);
   122	        }
   123	        EventBus bus = new EventBus(
   124	                name,
   125	                regionResolver.buildArn("events", region, "event-bus/" + name),
   126	                description,
   127	                Instant.now()
   128	        );
   129	        if (tags != null) {
   130	            bus.getTags().putAll(tags);
   131	        }
   132	        busStore.put(key, bus);
   133	        LOG.infov("Created event bus: {0} in region {1}", name, region);
   134	        return bus;
   135	    }
   136	
   137	    public void deleteEventBus(String name, String region) {
   138	        if ("default".equals(name)) {
   139	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException", "Cannot delete the default event bus.", 400);
   140	        }
   141	        String key = busKey(region, name);
   142	        busStore.get(key)
   143	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException",
   144	                        "EventBus not found: " + name, 404));
   145	        String rulePrefix = ruleKeyPrefix(region, name);
   146	        boolean hasRules = ruleStore.keys().stream().anyMatch(k -> k.startsWith(rulePrefix));
   147	        if (hasRules) {
   148	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException",
   149	                    "Cannot delete event bus with existing rules: " + name, 400);
   150	        }
   151	        busStore.delete(key);
   152	        LOG.infov("Deleted event bus: {0}", name);
   153	    }
   154	
   155	    public EventBus describeEventBus(String name, String region) {
   156	        String effectiveName = name == null || name.isBlank() ? "default" : name;
   157	        if ("default".equals(effectiveName)) {
   158	            return getOrCreateDefaultBus(region);
   159	        }
   160	        return busStore.get(busKey(region, effectiveName))
   161	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException",
   162	                        "EventBus not found: " + effectiveName, 404));
   163	    }
   164	
   165	    public List<EventBus> listEventBuses(String namePrefix, String region) {
   166	        getOrCreateDefaultBus(region);
   167	        String storagePrefix = "bus:" + region + ":";
   168	        List<EventBus> result = busStore.scan(k -> {
   169	            if (!k.startsWith(storagePrefix)) return false;
   170	            if (namePrefix == null || namePrefix.isBlank()) return true;
   171	            String busName = k.substring(storagePrefix.length());
   172	            return busName.startsWith(namePrefix);
   173	        });
   174	        return result;
   175	    }

   179	    public Rule putRule(String name, String busName, String eventPattern,
   180	                        String scheduleExpression, RuleState state, String description,
   181	                        String roleArn, Map<String, String> tags, String region) {
   182	        String effectiveBus = resolvedBusName(busName);
   183	        ensureBusExists(effectiveBus, region);
   184	
   185	        String key = ruleKey(region, effectiveBus, name);
   186	        Rule rule = ruleStore.get(key).orElse(new Rule());
   187	        rule.setName(name);
   188	        rule.setArn(regionResolver.buildArn("events", region, "rule/" + effectiveBus + "/" + name));
   189	        rule.setEventBusName(effectiveBus);
   190	        rule.setEventPattern(eventPattern);
   191	        rule.setScheduleExpression(scheduleExpression);
   192	        rule.setState(state != null ? state : RuleState.ENABLED);
   193	        rule.setDescription(description);
   194	        rule.setRoleArn(roleArn);
   195	        if (tags != null) {
   196	            rule.getTags().putAll(tags);
   197	        }
   198	        if (rule.getCreatedAt() == null) {
   199	            rule.setCreatedAt(Instant.now());
   200	        }
   201	        ruleStore.put(key, rule);
   202	        LOG.infov("Put rule: {0} on bus {1}", name, effectiveBus);
   203	        return rule;
   204	    }

   206	    public void deleteRule(String name, String busName, String region) {
   207	        String effectiveBus = resolvedBusName(busName);
   208	        String key = ruleKey(region, effectiveBus, name);
   209	        ruleStore.get(key)
   210	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException",
   211	                        "Rule not found: " + name, 404));
   212	        List<Target> targets = targetStore.get(key).orElse(List.of());
   213	        if (!targets.isEmpty()) {
   214	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException",
   215	                    "Rule still has targets. Remove targets before deleting the rule.", 400);
   216	        }
   217	        ruleStore.delete(key);
   218	        LOG.infov("Deleted rule: {0}", name);
   219	    }

   224	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException",
   225	                        "Rule not found: " + name, 404));

   228	    public List<Rule> listRules(String busName, String namePrefix, String region) {
   229	        String effectiveBus = resolvedBusName(busName);
   230	        String prefix = ruleKeyPrefix(region, effectiveBus);
   231	        return ruleStore.scan(k -> {
   232	            if (!k.startsWith(prefix)) return false;
   233	            if (namePrefix == null || namePrefix.isBlank()) return true;
   234	            String ruleName = k.substring(prefix.length());
   235	            return ruleName.startsWith(namePrefix);
   236	        });
   237	    }

   240	        String effectiveBus = resolvedBusName(busName);

   242	        Rule rule = ruleStore.get(key)
   243	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException",
   244	                        "Rule not found: " + name, 404));
   245	        rule.setState(RuleState.ENABLED);
   246	        ruleStore.put(key, rule);

   249	    public void disableRule(String name, String busName, String region) {
   250	        String effectiveBus = resolvedBusName(busName);
   251	        String key = ruleKey(region, effectiveBus, name);
   252	        Rule rule = ruleStore.get(key)
   253	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException",
   254	                        "Rule not found: " + name, 404));

   261	    public int putTargets(String ruleName, String busName, List<Target> newTargets, String region) {
   262	        String effectiveBus = resolvedBusName(busName);
   263	        String key = ruleKey(region, effectiveBus, ruleName);
   264	        ruleStore.get(key)
   265	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException",
   266	                        "Rule not found: " + ruleName, 404));
   267	        List<Target> existing = new ArrayList<>(targetStore.get(key).orElse(new ArrayList<>()));
   268	        for (Target newTarget : newTargets) {
   269	            existing.removeIf(t -> t.getId().equals(newTarget.getId()));
   270	            existing.add(newTarget);
   271	        }
   272	        targetStore.put(key, existing);
   273	        LOG.infov("Put {0} targets on rule {1}", newTargets.size(), ruleName);
   274	        return 0;
   275	    }

   277	    public record RemoveTargetsResult(int successfulCount, int failedCount) {}
   278	
   279	    public RemoveTargetsResult removeTargets(String ruleName, String busName,
   280	                                             List<String> ids, String region) {
   281	        String effectiveBus = resolvedBusName(busName);
   282	        String key = ruleKey(region, effectiveBus, ruleName);
   283	        List<Target> existing = new ArrayList<>(targetStore.get(key).orElse(new ArrayList<>()));
   284	        int removed = 0;
   285	        for (String id : ids) {
   286	            if (existing.removeIf(t -> t.getId().equals(id))) {
   287	                removed++;
   288	            }
   289	        }
   290	        targetStore.put(key, existing);
   291	        return new RemoveTargetsResult(removed, ids.size() - removed);
   292	    }

   294	    public List<Target> listTargetsByRule(String ruleName, String busName, String region) {
   295	        String effectiveBus = resolvedBusName(busName);
   296	        String key = ruleKey(region, effectiveBus, ruleName);
   297	        ruleStore.get(key)
   298	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException",
   299	                        "Rule not found: " + ruleName, 404));
   300	        return targetStore.get(key).orElse(List.of());
   301	    }

   304	
   305	    public record PutEventsResult(int failedCount, List<Map<String, String>> entries) {}
   306	
   307	    public PutEventsResult putEvents(List<Map<String, Object>> entries, String region) {
   308	        int failed = 0;
   309	        List<Map<String, String>> resultEntries = new ArrayList<>();
   310	
   311	        for (Map<String, Object> entry : entries) {
   312	            String eventBusNameRaw = (String) entry.get("EventBusName");
   313	            String effectiveBus = resolvedBusName(eventBusNameRaw);
   314	            String busStoreKey = busKey(region, effectiveBus);
   315	
   316	            if ("default".equals(effectiveBus)) {
   317	                getOrCreateDefaultBus(region);
   318	            } else if (busStore.get(busStoreKey).isEmpty()) {
   319	                failed++;
   320	                Map<String, String> errorEntry = new HashMap<>();
   321	                errorEntry.put("ErrorCode", "InvalidArgument");
   322	                errorEntry.put("ErrorMessage", "EventBus not found: " + effectiveBus);
   323	                resultEntries.add(errorEntry);
   324	                continue;
   325	            }
   326	
   327	            String eventId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
   328	            String rulePrefix = ruleKeyPrefix(region, effectiveBus);
   329	            List<Rule> matchedRules = ruleStore.scan(k ->
   330	                    k.startsWith(rulePrefix) && isRuleEnabled(k));
   331	
   332	            for (Rule rule : matchedRules) {
   333	                if (matchesPattern(entry, rule.getEventPattern())) {
   334	                    String ruleKey = ruleKey(region, effectiveBus, rule.getName());
   335	                    List<Target> targets = targetStore.get(ruleKey).orElse(List.of());
   336	                    String eventJson = buildEventEnvelope(entry, effectiveBus, eventId);
   337	                    for (Target target : targets) {
   338	                        invokeTarget(target, eventJson, region);
   339	                    }
   340	                }
   341	            }
   342	
   343	            Map<String, String> successEntry = new HashMap<>();
   344	            successEntry.put("EventId", eventId);
   345	            resultEntries.add(successEntry);
   346	        }
   347	
   348	        return new PutEventsResult(failed, resultEntries);
   349	    }

   355	            return true;

   354	        if (eventPattern == null || eventPattern.isBlank()) {
   355	            return true;
   356	        }
   357	        try {
   358	            JsonNode pattern = objectMapper.readTree(eventPattern);
   359	            JsonNode sourceField = pattern.get("source");
   360	            if (sourceField != null && sourceField.isArray()) {
   361	                String eventSource = (String) event.get("Source");
   362	                if (!matchesArrayField(sourceField, eventSource)) {
   363	                    return false;
   364	                }
   365	            }
   366	            JsonNode detailTypeField = pattern.get("detail-type");
   367	            if (detailTypeField != null && detailTypeField.isArray()) {
   368	                String eventDetailType = (String) event.get("DetailType");
   369	                if (!matchesArrayField(detailTypeField, eventDetailType)) {
   370	                    return false;
   371	                }
   372	            }
   373	            JsonNode detailPattern = pattern.get("detail");
   374	            if (detailPattern != null && detailPattern.isObject()) {
   375	                Object eventDetail = event.get("Detail");
   376	                String detailStr = eventDetail instanceof String s ? s : null;
   377	                if (detailStr == null) {
   378	                    return false;
   379	                }
   380	                JsonNode detailNode = objectMapper.readTree(detailStr);
   381	                var fields = detailPattern.fields();
   382	                while (fields.hasNext()) {
   383	                    var field = fields.next();
   384	                    JsonNode expected = field.getValue();
   385	                    JsonNode actual = detailNode.get(field.getKey());
   386	                    String actualStr = actual != null ? actual.asText(null) : null;
   387	                    if (expected.isArray() && !matchesArrayField(expected, actualStr)) {
   388	                        return false;
   389	                    }
   390	                }
   391	            }
   392	            return true;
   393	        } catch (Exception e) {
   394	            LOG.warnv("Failed to parse event pattern: {0}", e.getMessage());
   395	            return false;
   396	        }

   399	    private boolean matchesArrayField(JsonNode arrayNode, String value) {
   400	        if (value == null) return false;
   401	        for (JsonNode element : arrayNode) {
   402	            if (value.equals(element.asText())) {
   403	                return true;
   404	            }
   405	        }
   406	        return false;
   407	    }

   409	    // ──────────────────────────── Target Routing ────────────────────────────
   410	
   411	    private void invokeTarget(Target target, String eventJson, String region) {
   412	        String arn = target.getArn();
   413	        String payload = target.getInput() != null ? target.getInput() : eventJson;
   414	        try {
   415	            if (arn.contains(":lambda:") || arn.contains(":function:")) {
   416	                String fnName = arn.substring(arn.lastIndexOf(':') + 1);
   417	                String fnRegion = extractRegionFromArn(arn, region);
   418	                lambdaService.invoke(fnRegion, fnName, payload.getBytes(), InvocationType.Event);
   419	                LOG.debugv("EventBridge delivered to Lambda: {0}", arn);
   420	            } else if (arn.contains(":sqs:")) {
   421	                String queueUrl = sqsArnToUrl(arn);
   422	                sqsService.sendMessage(queueUrl, payload, 0);
   423	                LOG.debugv("EventBridge delivered to SQS: {0}", arn);
   424	            } else if (arn.contains(":sns:")) {
   425	                String topicRegion = extractRegionFromArn(arn, region);
   426	                snsService.publish(arn, null, payload, "EventBridge", topicRegion);
   427	                LOG.debugv("EventBridge delivered to SNS: {0}", arn);
   428	            } else {
   429	                LOG.warnv("EventBridge: unsupported target ARN type: {0}", arn);
   430	            }
   431	        } catch (Exception e) {
   432	            LOG.warnv("EventBridge failed to deliver to target {0}: {1}", arn, e.getMessage());
   433	        }
   434	    }

   436	    private String buildEventEnvelope(Map<String, Object> entry, String busName, String eventId) {
   437	        try {
   438	            String source = (String) entry.getOrDefault("Source", "");
   439	            String detailType = (String) entry.getOrDefault("DetailType", "");
   440	            String detail = (String) entry.getOrDefault("Detail", "{}");
   441	            ObjectNode node = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   442	            node.put("version", "0");
   443	            node.put("id", eventId);
   444	            node.put("source", source);
   445	            node.put("detail-type", detailType);
   446	            node.put("account", regionResolver.getAccountId());
   447	            node.put("time", Instant.now().toString());
   448	            node.put("region", regionResolver.getDefaultRegion());
   449	            node.putArray("resources");
   450	            node.set("detail", objectMapper.readTree(detail));
   451	            node.put("event-bus-name", busName);
   452	            return objectMapper.writeValueAsString(node);
   453	        } catch (Exception e) {
   454	            return "{}";
   455	        }
   456	    }

   460	    private boolean isRuleEnabled(String ruleStoreKey) {
   461	        return ruleStore.get(ruleStoreKey)
   462	                .map(r -> r.getState() == RuleState.ENABLED)
   463	                .orElse(false);
   464	    }

   466	    private void ensureBusExists(String busName, String region) {
   467	        if ("default".equals(busName)) {
   468	            getOrCreateDefaultBus(region);
   469	            return;
   470	        }
   471	        busStore.get(busKey(region, busName))
   472	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException",
   473	                        "EventBus not found: " + busName, 404));
   474	    }
   475	
   476	    private static String resolvedBusName(String busName) {
   477	        return (busName == null || busName.isBlank()) ? "default" : busName;
   478	    }
   479	
   480	    private static String busKey(String region, String name) {
   481	        return "bus:" + region + ":" + name;
   482	    }
   483	
   484	    private static String ruleKeyPrefix(String region, String busName) {
   485	        return "rule:" + region + ":" + busName + "/";
   486	    }
   487	
   488	    private static String ruleKey(String region, String busName, String ruleName) {
   489	        return ruleKeyPrefix(region, busName) + ruleName;
   490	    }
   491	
   492	    private static String extractRegionFromArn(String arn, String defaultRegion) {
   493	        String[] parts = arn.split(":");
   494	        return parts.length >= 4 && !parts[3].isEmpty() ? parts[3] : defaultRegion;
   495	    }

    28	public class EventBridgeHandler {
    29	
    30	    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(EventBridgeHandler.class);
    31	
    32	    private final EventBridgeService eventBridgeService;
    33	    private final ObjectMapper objectMapper;
    34	
    35	    @Inject
    36	    public EventBridgeHandler(EventBridgeService eventBridgeService, ObjectMapper objectMapper) {
    37	        this.eventBridgeService = eventBridgeService;
    38	        this.objectMapper = objectMapper;
    39	    }
    40	
    41	    public Response handle(String action, JsonNode request, String region) {
    42	        LOG.debugv("EventBridge action: {0}", action);
    43	
    44	        try {
    45	            return switch (action) {
    46	                case "CreateEventBus" -> handleCreateEventBus(request, region);
    47	                case "DeleteEventBus" -> handleDeleteEventBus(request, region);
    48	                case "DescribeEventBus" -> handleDescribeEventBus(request, region);
    49	                case "ListEventBuses" -> handleListEventBuses(request, region);
    50	                case "PutRule" -> handlePutRule(request, region);
    51	                case "DeleteRule" -> handleDeleteRule(request, region);
    52	                case "DescribeRule" -> handleDescribeRule(request, region);
    53	                case "ListRules" -> handleListRules(request, region);
    54	                case "EnableRule" -> handleEnableRule(request, region);
    55	                case "DisableRule" -> handleDisableRule(request, region);
    56	                case "PutTargets" -> handlePutTargets(request, region);
    57	                case "RemoveTargets" -> handleRemoveTargets(request, region);
    58	                case "ListTargetsByRule" -> handleListTargetsByRule(request, region);
    59	                case "PutEvents" -> handlePutEvents(request, region);
    60	                default -> Response.status(400)
    61	                        .entity(new AwsErrorResponse("UnsupportedOperation", "Operation " + action + " is not supported."))
    62	                        .build();
    63	            };
    64	        } catch (AwsException e) {
    65	            return Response.status(e.getHttpStatus())
    66	                    .entity(new AwsErrorResponse(e.getErrorCode(), e.getMessage()))
    67	                    .build();
    68	        } catch (Exception e) {
    69	            LOG.errorv("EventBridge error processing action {0}: {1}", action, e.getMessage());
    70	            return Response.status(500)
    71	                    .entity(new AwsErrorResponse("InternalFailure", e.getMessage()))
    72	                    .build();
    73	        }
    74	    }
    75	
    76	    private Response handleCreateEventBus(JsonNode request, String region) {
    77	        String name = request.path("Name").asText(null);
    78	        String description = request.path("Description").asText(null);
    79	        Map<String, String> tags = parseTagsArray(request.path("Tags"));
    80	        EventBus bus = eventBridgeService.createEventBus(name, description, tags, region);
    81	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
    82	        response.put("EventBusArn", bus.getArn());
    83	        return Response.ok(response).build();
    84	    }
    85	
    86	    private Response handleDeleteEventBus(JsonNode request, String region) {
    87	        String name = request.path("Name").asText(null);
    88	        eventBridgeService.deleteEventBus(name, region);
    89	        return Response.ok(objectMapper.createObjectNode()).build();
    90	    }
    91	
    92	    private Response handleDescribeEventBus(JsonNode request, String region) {
    93	        String name = request.path("Name").asText(null);
    94	        EventBus bus = eventBridgeService.describeEventBus(name, region);
    95	        return Response.ok(buildBusNode(bus)).build();
    96	    }
    97	
    98	    private Response handleListEventBuses(JsonNode request, String region) {
    99	        String namePrefix = request.path("NamePrefix").asText(null);
   100	        List<EventBus> buses = eventBridgeService.listEventBuses(namePrefix, region);
   101	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   102	        ArrayNode busesArray = response.putArray("EventBuses");
   103	        for (EventBus bus : buses) {
   104	            busesArray.add(buildBusNode(bus));
   105	        }
   106	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   107	    }
   108	
   109	    private Response handlePutRule(JsonNode request, String region) {
   110	        String name = request.path("Name").asText(null);
   111	        String busName = request.path("EventBusName").asText(null);
   112	        String eventPattern = request.path("EventPattern").asText(null);
   113	        String scheduleExpression = request.path("ScheduleExpression").asText(null);
   114	        RuleState state = parseRuleState(request.path("State").asText(null));
   115	        String description = request.path("Description").asText(null);
   116	        String roleArn = request.path("RoleArn").asText(null);
   117	        Map<String, String> tags = parseTagsArray(request.path("Tags"));
   118	        Rule rule = eventBridgeService.putRule(name, busName, eventPattern, scheduleExpression,
   119	                state, description, roleArn, tags, region);
   120	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   121	        response.put("RuleArn", rule.getArn());
   122	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   123	    }
   124	
   125	    private Response handleDeleteRule(JsonNode request, String region) {
   126	        String name = request.path("Name").asText(null);
   127	        String busName = request.path("EventBusName").asText(null);
   128	        eventBridgeService.deleteRule(name, busName, region);
   129	        return Response.ok(objectMapper.createObjectNode()).build();
   130	    }
   131	
   132	    private Response handleDescribeRule(JsonNode request, String region) {
   133	        String name = request.path("Name").asText(null);
   134	        String busName = request.path("EventBusName").asText(null);
   135	        Rule rule = eventBridgeService.describeRule(name, busName, region);
   136	        return Response.ok(buildRuleNode(rule)).build();
   137	    }
   138	
   139	    private Response handleListRules(JsonNode request, String region) {
   140	        String busName = request.path("EventBusName").asText(null);
   141	        String namePrefix = request.path("NamePrefix").asText(null);
   142	        List<Rule> rules = eventBridgeService.listRules(busName, namePrefix, region);
   143	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   144	        ArrayNode rulesArray = response.putArray("Rules");
   145	        for (Rule rule : rules) {
   146	            rulesArray.add(buildRuleNode(rule));
   147	        }
   148	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   149	    }
   150	
   151	    private Response handleEnableRule(JsonNode request, String region) {
   152	        String name = request.path("Name").asText(null);
   153	        String busName = request.path("EventBusName").asText(null);
   154	        eventBridgeService.enableRule(name, busName, region);
   155	        return Response.ok(objectMapper.createObjectNode()).build();
   156	    }
   157	
   158	    private Response handleDisableRule(JsonNode request, String region) {
   159	        String name = request.path("Name").asText(null);
   160	        String busName = request.path("EventBusName").asText(null);
   161	        eventBridgeService.disableRule(name, busName, region);
   162	        return Response.ok(objectMapper.createObjectNode()).build();
   163	    }
   164	
   165	    private Response handlePutTargets(JsonNode request, String region) {
   166	        String ruleName = request.path("Rule").asText(null);
   167	        String busName = request.path("EventBusName").asText(null);
   168	        List<Target> targets = new ArrayList<>();
   169	        JsonNode targetsNode = request.path("Targets");
   170	        if (targetsNode.isArray()) {
   171	            for (JsonNode t : targetsNode) {
   172	                String input = t.path("Input").asText("");
   173	                String inputPath = t.path("InputPath").asText("");
   174	                Target target = new Target(
   175	                        t.path("Id").asText(null),
   176	                        t.path("Arn").asText(null),
   177	                        input.isEmpty() ? null : input,
   178	                        inputPath.isEmpty() ? null : inputPath
   179	                );
   180	                targets.add(target);
   181	            }
   182	        }
   183	        int failed = eventBridgeService.putTargets(ruleName, busName, targets, region);
   184	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   185	        response.put("FailedEntryCount", failed);
   186	        response.putArray("FailedEntries");
   187	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   188	    }
   189	
   190	    private Response handleRemoveTargets(JsonNode request, String region) {
   191	        String ruleName = request.path("Rule").asText(null);
   192	        String busName = request.path("EventBusName").asText(null);
   193	        List<String> ids = new ArrayList<>();
   194	        JsonNode idsNode = request.path("Ids");
   195	        if (idsNode.isArray()) {
   196	            for (JsonNode id : idsNode) {
   197	                ids.add(id.asText());
   198	            }
   199	        }
   200	        EventBridgeService.RemoveTargetsResult result =
   201	                eventBridgeService.removeTargets(ruleName, busName, ids, region);
   202	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   203	        response.put("SuccessfulEntryCount", result.successfulCount());
   204	        response.put("FailedEntryCount", result.failedCount());
   205	        response.putArray("SuccessfulEntries");
   206	        response.putArray("FailedEntries");
   207	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   208	    }
   209	
   210	    private Response handleListTargetsByRule(JsonNode request, String region) {
   211	        String ruleName = request.path("Rule").asText(null);
   212	        String busName = request.path("EventBusName").asText(null);
   213	        List<Target> targets = eventBridgeService.listTargetsByRule(ruleName, busName, region);
   214	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   215	        ArrayNode targetsArray = response.putArray("Targets");
   216	        for (Target t : targets) {
   217	            ObjectNode node = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   218	            node.put("Id", t.getId());
   219	            node.put("Arn", t.getArn());
   220	            if (t.getInput() != null) {
   221	                node.put("Input", t.getInput());
   222	            }
   223	            if (t.getInputPath() != null) {
   224	                node.put("InputPath", t.getInputPath());
   225	            }
   226	            targetsArray.add(node);
   227	        }
   228	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   229	    }
   230	
   231	    private Response handlePutEvents(JsonNode request, String region) {
   232	        List<Map<String, Object>> entries = new ArrayList<>();
   233	        JsonNode entriesNode = request.path("Entries");
   234	        if (entriesNode.isArray()) {
   235	            for (JsonNode entryNode : entriesNode) {
   236	                Map<String, Object> entry = new HashMap<>();
   237	                if (!entryNode.path("EventBusName").isMissingNode()) {
   238	                    entry.put("EventBusName", entryNode.path("EventBusName").asText(null));
   239	                }
   240	                if (!entryNode.path("Source").isMissingNode()) {
   241	                    entry.put("Source", entryNode.path("Source").asText(null));
   242	                }
   243	                if (!entryNode.path("DetailType").isMissingNode()) {
   244	                    entry.put("DetailType", entryNode.path("DetailType").asText(null));
   245	                }
   246	                if (!entryNode.path("Detail").isMissingNode()) {
   247	                    entry.put("Detail", entryNode.path("Detail").asText(null));
   248	                }
   249	                entries.add(entry);
   250	            }
   251	        }
   252	        EventBridgeService.PutEventsResult result = eventBridgeService.putEvents(entries, region);
   253	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   254	        response.put("FailedEntryCount", result.failedCount());
   255	        ArrayNode resultEntries = response.putArray("Entries");
   256	        for (Map<String, String> entry : result.entries()) {
   257	            ObjectNode node = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   258	            entry.forEach(node::put);
   259	            resultEntries.add(node);
   260	        }
   261	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   262	    }
   263	
   264	    // ──────────────────────────── Helpers ────────────────────────────
   265	
   266	    private ObjectNode buildBusNode(EventBus bus) {
   267	        ObjectNode node = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   268	        node.put("Name", bus.getName());
   269	        node.put("Arn", bus.getArn());
   270	        if (bus.getDescription() != null) {
   271	            node.put("Description", bus.getDescription());
   272	        }
   273	        if (bus.getCreatedTime() != null) {
   274	            node.put("CreationTime", bus.getCreatedTime().getEpochSecond());
   275	        }
   276	        return node;
   277	    }
   278	
   279	    private ObjectNode buildRuleNode(Rule rule) {
   280	        ObjectNode node = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   281	        node.put("Name", rule.getName());
   282	        node.put("Arn", rule.getArn());
   283	        node.put("EventBusName", rule.getEventBusName());
   284	        node.put("State", rule.getState().name());
   285	        if (rule.getEventPattern() != null) {
   286	            node.put("EventPattern", rule.getEventPattern());
   287	        }
   288	        if (rule.getScheduleExpression() != null) {
   289	            node.put("ScheduleExpression", rule.getScheduleExpression());
   290	        }
   291	        if (rule.getDescription() != null) {
   292	            node.put("Description", rule.getDescription());
   293	        }
   294	        if (rule.getRoleArn() != null) {
   295	            node.put("RoleArn", rule.getRoleArn());
   296	        }
   297	        return node;
   298	    }
   299	
   300	    private RuleState parseRuleState(String state) {
   301	        if (state == null || state.isBlank()) {
   302	            return RuleState.ENABLED;
   303	        }
   304	        return switch (state.toUpperCase()) {
   305	            case "DISABLED" -> RuleState.DISABLED;
   306	            default -> RuleState.ENABLED;
   307	        };
   308	    }
   309	
   310	    private Map<String, String> parseTagsArray(JsonNode tagsNode) {
   311	        Map<String, String> tags = new HashMap<>();
   312	        if (tagsNode != null && tagsNode.isArray()) {
   313	            for (JsonNode tag : tagsNode) {
   314	                String key = tag.path("Key").asText(null);
   315	                String value = tag.path("Value").asText(null);
   316	                if (key != null) {
   317	                    tags.put(key, value);
   318	                }
   319	            }
   320	        }
   321	        return tags;
   322	    }
   323	}

        if (eventPattern == null || eventPattern.isBlank()) {
            return true;
        }
        try {
            JsonNode pattern = objectMapper.readTree(eventPattern);
            JsonNode sourceField = pattern.get("source");
            if (sourceField != null && sourceField.isArray()) {
                String eventSource = (String) event.get("Source");
                if (!matchesArrayField(sourceField, eventSource)) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
            JsonNode detailTypeField = pattern.get("detail-type");
            if (detailTypeField != null && detailTypeField.isArray()) {
                String eventDetailType = (String) event.get("DetailType");
                if (!matchesArrayField(detailTypeField, eventDetailType)) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
            JsonNode resourcesField = pattern.get("resources");
            if (resourcesField != null && resourcesField.isArray()) {
                if (!matchesResourcesField(resourcesField, event.get("Resources"))) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
            JsonNode detailPattern = pattern.get("detail");
            if (detailPattern != null && detailPattern.isObject()) {
                Object eventDetail = event.get("Detail");

                    String actualStr = actual != null ? actual.asText(null) : null;
                    if (expected.isArray() && !matchesArrayField(expected, actualStr)) {
                        return false;
                    }
                }

            return true;

            LOG.warnv("Failed to parse event pattern: {0}", e.getMessage());
            return false;
        }
    }

    private boolean matchesResourcesField(JsonNode patternArray, Object eventResources) {
        if (eventResources == null) {
            return false;
        }
        if (eventResources instanceof List<?> resourcesList) {
            for (Object resource : resourcesList) {
                String resourceStr = resource != null ? resource.toString() : null;
                if (matchesArrayField(patternArray, resourceStr)) {
                    return true;
                }
            }
        }
        return false;

   360	            JsonNode sourceField = pattern.get("source");
   361	            if (sourceField != null && sourceField.isArray()) {
   362	                String eventSource = (String) event.get("Source");
   363	                if (!matchesArrayField(sourceField, eventSource)) {
   364	                    return false;
   365	                }
   366	            }
   367	            JsonNode detailTypeField = pattern.get("detail-type");
   368	            if (detailTypeField != null && detailTypeField.isArray()) {
   369	                String eventDetailType = (String) event.get("DetailType");
   370	                if (!matchesArrayField(detailTypeField, eventDetailType)) {
   371	                    return false;
   372	                }
   373	            }
   374	            JsonNode resourcesField = pattern.get("resources");
   375	            if (resourcesField != null && resourcesField.isArray()) {
   376	                if (!matchesResourcesField(resourcesField, event.get("Resources"))) {
   377	                    return false;
   378	                }
   379	            }
   380	            JsonNode detailPattern = pattern.get("detail");
   381	            if (detailPattern != null && detailPattern.isObject()) {
   382	                Object eventDetail = event.get("Detail");
   383	                String detailStr = eventDetail instanceof String s ? s : null;
   384	                if (detailStr == null) {
   385	                    return false;
   386	                }
   387	                JsonNode detailNode = objectMapper.readTree(detailStr);
   388	                var fields = detailPattern.fields();
   389	                while (fields.hasNext()) {
   390	                    var field = fields.next();
   391	                    JsonNode expected = field.getValue();
   392	                    JsonNode actual = detailNode.get(field.getKey());
   393	                    String actualStr = actual != null ? actual.asText(null) : null;
   394	                    if (expected.isArray() && !matchesArrayField(expected, actualStr)) {
   395	                        return false;
   396	                    }
   397	                }
   398	            }
   399	            return true;
   400	        } catch (Exception e) {
   401	            LOG.warnv("Failed to parse event pattern: {0}", e.getMessage());
   402	            return false;
   403	        }
   404	    }
   405	
   406	    private boolean matchesResourcesField(JsonNode patternArray, Object eventResources) {
   407	        if (eventResources == null) {
   408	            return false;
   409	        }
   410	        if (eventResources instanceof List<?> resourcesList) {
   411	            for (Object resource : resourcesList) {
   412	                String resourceStr = resource != null ? resource.toString() : null;
   413	                if (matchesArrayField(patternArray, resourceStr)) {
   414	                    return true;
   415	                }
   416	            }
   417	        }
   418	        return false;
   419	    }
   420	
   421	    private boolean matchesArrayField(JsonNode arrayNode, String value) {
   422	        if (value == null) return false;

   352	    // ──────────────────────────── Pattern Matching ────────────────────────────
   353	
   354	    boolean matchesPattern(Map<String, Object> event, String eventPattern) {
   355	        if (eventPattern == null || eventPattern.isBlank()) {
   356	            return true;
   357	        }
   358	        try {
   359	            JsonNode pattern = objectMapper.readTree(eventPattern);
   360	            JsonNode sourceField = pattern.get("source");
   361	            if (sourceField != null && sourceField.isArray()) {
   362	                String eventSource = (String) event.get("Source");
   363	                if (!matchesArrayField(sourceField, eventSource)) {
   364	                    return false;
   365	                }
   366	            }
   367	            JsonNode detailTypeField = pattern.get("detail-type");
   368	            if (detailTypeField != null && detailTypeField.isArray()) {
   369	                String eventDetailType = (String) event.get("DetailType");
   370	                if (!matchesArrayField(detailTypeField, eventDetailType)) {
   371	                    return false;
   372	                }
   373	            }
   374	            JsonNode resourcesField = pattern.get("resources");
   375	            if (resourcesField != null && resourcesField.isArray()) {
   376	                if (!matchesResourcesField(resourcesField, event.get("Resources"))) {
   377	                    return false;
   378	                }
   379	            }
   380	            JsonNode detailPattern = pattern.get("detail");
   381	            if (detailPattern != null && detailPattern.isObject()) {
   382	                Object eventDetail = event.get("Detail");
   383	                String detailStr = eventDetail instanceof String s ? s : null;
   384	                if (detailStr == null) {
   385	                    return false;
   386	                }
   387	                JsonNode detailNode = objectMapper.readTree(detailStr);
   388	                var fields = detailPattern.fields();
   389	                while (fields.hasNext()) {
   390	                    var field = fields.next();
   391	                    JsonNode expected = field.getValue();
   392	                    JsonNode actual = detailNode.get(field.getKey());
   393	                    String actualStr = actual != null ? actual.asText(null) : null;
   394	                    if (expected.isArray() && !matchesArrayField(expected, actualStr)) {
   395	                        return false;
   396	                    }
   397	                }
   398	            }
   399	            return true;
   400	        } catch (Exception e) {
   401	            LOG.warnv("Failed to parse event pattern: {0}", e.getMessage());
   402	            return false;
   403	        }
   404	    }
   405	
   406	    private boolean matchesResourcesField(JsonNode patternArray, Object eventResources) {
   407	        if (eventResources == null) {
   408	            return false;
   409	        }
   410	        if (eventResources instanceof List<?> resourcesList) {
   411	            for (Object resource : resourcesList) {
   412	                String resourceStr = resource != null ? resource.toString() : null;
   413	                if (matchesArrayField(patternArray, resourceStr)) {
   414	                    return true;
   415	                }
   416	            }
   417	        }
   418	        return false;
   419	    }
   420	
   421	    private boolean matchesArrayField(JsonNode arrayNode, String value) {
   422	        if (value == null) return false;
   423	        for (JsonNode element : arrayNode) {
   424	            if (value.equals(element.asText())) {
   425	                return true;

   231	    private Response handlePutEvents(JsonNode request, String region) {
   232	        List<Map<String, Object>> entries = new ArrayList<>();
   233	        JsonNode entriesNode = request.path("Entries");
   234	        if (entriesNode.isArray()) {
   235	            for (JsonNode entryNode : entriesNode) {
   236	                Map<String, Object> entry = new HashMap<>();
   237	                if (!entryNode.path("EventBusName").isMissingNode()) {
   238	                    entry.put("EventBusName", entryNode.path("EventBusName").asText(null));
   239	                }
   240	                if (!entryNode.path("Source").isMissingNode()) {
   241	                    entry.put("Source", entryNode.path("Source").asText(null));
   242	                }
   243	                if (!entryNode.path("DetailType").isMissingNode()) {
   244	                    entry.put("DetailType", entryNode.path("DetailType").asText(null));
   245	                }
   246	                if (!entryNode.path("Detail").isMissingNode()) {
   247	                    entry.put("Detail", entryNode.path("Detail").asText(null));
   248	                }
   249	                if (!entryNode.path("Resources").isMissingNode()) {
   250	                    JsonNode resourcesNode = entryNode.path("Resources");
   251	                    if (resourcesNode.isArray()) {
   252	                        List<String> resources = new ArrayList<>();
   253	                        for (JsonNode res : resourcesNode) {
   254	                            resources.add(res.asText());
   255	                        }
   256	                        entry.put("Resources", resources);
   257	                    }
   258	                }
   259	                entries.add(entry);
   260	            }
   261	        }
   262	        EventBridgeService.PutEventsResult result = eventBridgeService.putEvents(entries, region);
   263	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   264	        response.put("FailedEntryCount", result.failedCount());
   265	        ArrayNode resultEntries = response.putArray("Entries");
   266	        for (Map<String, String> entry : result.entries()) {
   267	            ObjectNode node = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   268	            entry.forEach(node::put);
   269	            resultEntries.add(node);
   270	        }
   271	        return Response.ok(response).build();
